0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou must create an environment which contains all the objects described in this section. You can display the objects in any way you wish.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e1 Roads\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou will create two roads which cross each other to create an intersection. Each road will have \u003cstrong\u003eone lane\u003c/strong\u003e in each direction.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTraffic entering the intersection will be able to select a route by:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eturning left\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eturning right\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003econtinuing on straight\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-shell-session notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\" →                                     → →\n     _______________             _______________\n                    |     |     |\n                    |     |     |\n                    |     |     |\n                    |     |     |\n                    |     |     |\n                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\n                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\n                        South\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                        North\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e     _______________|     |     |_______________\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e     ← ←                                     ← ←\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eEast ---------------             --------------- West\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e     → →                                     → →\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e     _______________             _______________\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |     |     |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e                        South\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e2 Traffic lights\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTraffic lights are signaling devices positioned at road intersections that follow a universal color code. We all know the normal colors for traffic lights, but for this exercise, your traffic lights will only have \u003cstrong\u003ered\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003egreen\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou will position those traffic lights at the point where each lane enters the intersection.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can implement any algorithm you choose to control the traffic lights system, but bear in mind that \u003cstrong\u003etraffic congestion should remain below the lane’s maximum capacity\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDynamic Congestion Rule:\u003c/strong\u003e\nThe maximum allowed queue length for each lane is calculated based on the lane’s physical length, vehicle length, and safety gap between vehicles:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"capacity = floor(lane_length / (vehicle_length + safety_gap))\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecapacity = floor(lane_length / (vehicle_length + safety_gap))\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhere:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003elane_length\u003c/code\u003e: Distance from the stop line to the vehicle spawn point\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evehicle_length\u003c/code\u003e: Approximate car length in simulation units (e.g., pixels or meters)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003esafety_gap\u003c/code\u003e: Minimum safe distance between vehicles\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf the number of vehicles in a lane reaches this capacity, the traffic light logic should adjust (e.g., extend green time for that lane) to prevent overflow.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe primary function of your traffic light system is to avoid collisions between vehicles passing through the intersection, while dynamically adapting to congestion.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e3. Vehicles\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"  ______\n /|_||_\\`.__\n=`-(_)--(_)-'\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e  ______\n /|_||_\\`.__\n=`-(_)--(_)-'\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe vehicles traveling through your capital city's new junction must follow these rules:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVehicles must be painted in a color which illustrates the route they will follow. The colors are up to you to decide, and your choices will need to be made available during the audit of the raid. For example, all cars which make a right turn could be painted yellow. It's really up to you though.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIt is not possible for the vehicle to change its selected route.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEach vehicle must have a fixed velocity.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eA safety distance from other vehicles must be maintained. If one vehicle stops, the following vehicle must also stop before it gets too close to the stationary vehicle in front.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVehicles must stop if the traffic light is red and proceed otherwise.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThere are no other vehicle types with special privileges. road_intersection","","### Objectives","","Traffic, traffic, traffic...","","You will need to solve the traffic problem in your capital city. Your objective will be to create a traffic control strategy, and visualize it with a simulation.","","It is up to you to decide which library and file system you want to use in order to create this simulation, but we recommend that you use the [sdl2](https://docs.rs/sdl2/0.34.3/sdl2/) library.","","### Instructions","","#### **Environment and Rules**","","You must create an environment which contains all the objects described in this section. You can display the objects in any way you wish.","","**1 Roads**","","You will create two roads which cross each other to create an intersection. Each road will have **one lane** in each direction.","","Traffic entering the intersection will be able to select a route by:","","- turning left","- turning right","- continuing on straight","","```console","                        North","                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |","                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","     _______________|     |     |_______________","     ← ←                                     ← ←","East ---------------             --------------- West","     → →                                     → →","     _______________             _______________","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |     |     |","                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |","                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |","                        South","```","","**2 Traffic lights**","","Traffic lights are signaling devices positioned at road intersections that follow a universal color code. We all know the normal colors for traffic lights, but for this exercise, your traffic lights will only have **red** and **green**.","","You will position those traffic lights at the point where each lane enters the intersection.","","You can implement any algorithm you choose to control the traffic lights system, but bear in mind that **traffic congestion should remain below the lane’s maximum capacity**.","","\u003e **Dynamic Congestion Rule:**","\u003e The maximum allowed queue length for each lane is calculated based on the lane’s physical length, vehicle length, and safety gap between vehicles:","\u003e","\u003e ```","\u003e capacity = floor(lane_length / (vehicle_length + safety_gap))","\u003e ```","\u003e","\u003e Where:","\u003e","\u003e - `lane_length`: Distance from the stop line to the vehicle spawn point","\u003e - `vehicle_length`: Approximate car length in simulation units (e.g., pixels or meters)","\u003e - `safety_gap`: Minimum safe distance between vehicles","\u003e","\u003e If the number of vehicles in a lane reaches this capacity, the traffic light logic should adjust (e.g., extend green time for that lane) to prevent overflow.","","The primary function of your traffic light system is to avoid collisions between vehicles passing through the intersection, while dynamically adapting to congestion.","","**3. Vehicles**","","```","  ______"," /|_||_\\`.__","=`-(_)--(_)-'","```","","The vehicles traveling through your capital city's new junction must follow these rules:","","- Vehicles must be painted in a color which illustrates the route they will follow. The colors are up to you to decide, and your choices will need to be made available during the audit of the raid. For example, all cars which make a right turn could be painted yellow. It's really up to you though.","","- It is not possible for the vehicle to change its selected route.","","- Each vehicle must have a fixed velocity.","","- A safety distance from other vehicles must be maintained. If one vehicle stops, the following vehicle must also stop before it gets too close to the stationary vehicle in front.","","- Vehicles must stop if the traffic light is red and proceed otherwise.","","- There are no other vehicle types with special privileges. You can consider that there are no emergency vehicles in your capital city.","","---","","#### **Commands**","","You will use your keyboard to spawn vehicles for your simulation. You will use the arrow keys to spawn a vehicle on the appropriate side of the road, and with a random route.","","- **`↑` Up:** moves towards the intersection **from the south.**","- **`↓` Down:** moves towards the intersection **from the north.**","- **`→` Right:** moves towards the intersection **from the west.**","- **`←` Left:** moves towards the intersection **from the east.**","- **`r`:** moves towards the intersection **from a random direction.**","- **`Esc` Escape:** ends the simulation.","","\u003e It must not be possible to use the keyboard to spam the creation of vehicles; they must be created with a safe distance between them.","","\u003e A safe distance is any distance which enables the vehicles to avoid crashing into each other.","","### Example","","You can see an example for road_intersection [here](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6B0-ZBET6mo).","","### Bonus","","You can implement the following optional features:","","- Vehicle and traffic light animations, and image rendering. You can find some cool assets here:","  - [limezu](https://limezu.itch.io/)","  - [finalbossblue](http://finalbossblues.com/timefantasy/free-graphics/).","  - [spriters-resource](https://www.spriters-resource.com/).","","### Notions","","- https://docs.rs/sdl2/0.34.3/sdl2/"],"stylingDirectives":[[[0,20,"pl-mh"],[3,20,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,14,"pl-mh"],[4,14,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[],[],[[142,143,"pl-s"],[147,148,"pl-s"],[148,149,"pl-s"],[149,182,"pl-corl"],[182,183,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,16,"pl-mh"],[4,16,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,30,"pl-mh"],[5,30,"pl-en"],[5,7,"pl-s"],[28,30,"pl-s"]],[],[],[],[[0,2,"pl-s"],[9,11,"pl-s"]],[],[[96,98,"pl-s"],[106,108,"pl-s"]],[],[],[],[[0,1,"pl-v"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"]],[[0,1,"pl-v"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,10,"pl-en"]],[[0,29,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,48,"pl-c1"]],[[0,48,"pl-c1"]],[[0,53,"pl-c1"]],[[0,48,"pl-c1"]],[[0,48,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,33,"pl-c1"]],[[0,29,"pl-c1"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,2,"pl-s"],[18,20,"pl-s"]],[],[[214,216,"pl-s"],[219,221,"pl-s"],[226,228,"pl-s"],[233,235,"pl-s"]],[],[],[],[[103,105,"pl-s"],[171,173,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,30,"pl-ent"],[0,2,"pl-ent"],[2,4,"pl-s"],[28,30,"pl-s"]],[[0,148,"pl-ent"],[0,2,"pl-ent"]],[[0,1,"pl-ent"],[0,1,"pl-ent"]],[[0,5,"pl-ent"],[0,2,"pl-ent"],[2,5,"pl-s"],[5,5,"pl-c1"]],[[0,63,"pl-ent"],[0,63,"pl-c1"]],[[0,5,"pl-ent"],[0,5,"pl-c1"]],[[0,1,"pl-ent"],[0,1,"pl-c1"]],[[0,8,"pl-ent"],[0,8,"pl-c1"]],[[0,1,"pl-ent"],[0,1,"pl-c1"]],[[0,73,"pl-ent"],[0,73,"pl-c1"]],[[0,89,"pl-ent"],[0,89,"pl-c1"]],[[0,56,"pl-ent"],[0,56,"pl-c1"]],[[0,1,"pl-ent"],[0,1,"pl-c1"]],[[0,159,"pl-ent"],[0,159,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-ent"],[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,165,"pl-ent"],[0,165,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-ent"],[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,15,"pl-ent"],[0,15,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-ent"],[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,3,"pl-ent"],[0,0,"pl-c1"],[0,3,"pl-s"]],[[0,0,"pl-ent"],[0,8,"pl-ms"]],[[3,4,"pl-s"],[6,7,"pl-s"],[7,9,"pl-c1"],[10,12,"pl-s"]],[[4,5,"pl-s"],[9,10,"pl-s"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,3,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,88,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,298,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,66,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"]],[[0,42,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl- class="BlobContent-module__blobContentSection__VOgZq BlobContent-module__blobContentSectionMarkdown__mPLOK" style="margin-top:46px"><div class="js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned BlobContent-module__markdownBlob__T8jpG" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">road_intersection</h2><a id="user-content-road_intersection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: road_intersection" href="#road_intersection"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Objectives</h3><a id="user-content-objectives" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Objectives" href="#objectives"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Traffic, traffic, traffic...</p>
<p dir="auto">You will need to solve the traffic problem in your capital city. Your objective will be to create a traffic control strategy, and visualize it with a simulation.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is up to you to decide which library and file system you want to use in order to create this simulation, but we recommend that you use the <a href="https://docs.rs/sdl2/0.34.3/sdl2/" rel="nofollow">sdl2</a> library.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Instructions</h3><a id="user-content-instructions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Instructions" href="#instructions"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Environment and Rules</strong></h4><a id="user-content-environment-and-rules" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment and Rules" href="#environment-and-rules"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You must create an environment which contains all the objects described in this section. You can display the objects in any way you wish.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>1 Roads</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">You will create two roads which cross each other to create an intersection. Each road will have <strong>one lane</strong> in each direction.</p>
<p dir="auto">Traffic entering the intersection will be able to select a route by:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>turning left</li>
<li>turning right</li>
<li>continuing on straight</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-shell-session notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                        North
                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |
                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |

                    |     |     |

                    |     |     |

     ← ←                                     ← ←
East ---------------             --------------- West
     → →                                     → →
     _______________             _______________
                    |     |     |

                        South"><pre><span class="pl-c1">                        North</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |     |     |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |     |     |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |     |     |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                    |     |     |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">     _______________|     |     |_______________</span>

<span class="pl-c1">                    |  ↓  |  ↑  |</span>
<span class="pl-c1">                        South</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>2 Traffic lights</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Traffic lights are signaling devices positioned at road intersections that follow a universal color code. We all know the normal colors for traffic lights, but for this exercise, your traffic lights will only have <strong>red</strong> and <strong>green</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">You will position those traffic lights at the point where each lane enters the intersection.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can implement any algorithm you choose to control the traffic lights system, but bear in mind that <strong>traffic congestion should remain below the lane’s maximum capacity</strong>.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Dynamic Congestion Rule:</strong>
The maximum allowed queue length for each lane is calculated based on the lane’s physical length, vehicle length, and safety gap between vehicles:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="capacity = floor(lane_length / (vehicle_length + safety_gap))"><pre class="notranslate"><code>capacity = floor(lane_length / (vehicle_length + safety_gap))
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Where:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>lane_length</code>: Distance from the stop line to the vehicle spawn point</li>
<li><code>vehicle_length</code>: Approximate car length in simulation units (e.g., pixels or meters)</li>
<li><code>safety_gap</code>: Minimum safe distance between vehicles</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If the number of vehicles in a lane reaches this capacity, the traffic light logic should adjust (e.g., extend green time for that lane) to prevent overflow.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">The primary function of your traffic light system is to avoid collisions between vehicles passing through the intersection, while dynamically adapting to congestion.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>3. Vehicles</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  ______
 /|_||_\`.__
=`-(_)--(_)-'"><pre class="notranslate"><code>  ______
 /|_||_\`.__
=`-(_)--(_)-'
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The vehicles traveling through your capital city's new junction must follow these rules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Vehicles must be painted in a color which illustrates the route they will follow. The colors are up to you to decide, and your choices will need to be made available during the audit of the raid. For example, all cars which make a right turn could be painted yellow. It's really up to you though.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">It is not possible for the vehicle to change its selected route.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Each vehicle must have a fixed velocity.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">A safety distance from other vehicles must be maintained. If one vehicle stops, the following vehicle must also stop before it gets too close to the stationary vehicle in front.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Vehicles must stop if the traffic light is red and proceed otherwise.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">There are no other vehicle types with special privileges. You can consider that there are no emergency vehicles in your capital city.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Commands</strong></h4><a id="user-content-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Commands" href="#commands"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You will use your keyboard to spawn vehicles for your simulation. You will use the arrow keys to spawn a vehicle on the appropriate side of the road, and with a random route.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>↑</code> Up:</strong> moves towards the intersection <strong>from the south.</strong></li>
<li><strong><code>↓</code> Down:</strong> moves towards the intersection <strong>from the north.</strong></li>
<li><strong><code>→</code> Right:</strong> moves towards the intersection <strong>from the west.</strong></li>
<li><strong><code>←</code> Left:</strong> moves towards the intersection <strong>from the east.</strong></li>
<li><strong><code>r</code>:</strong> moves towards the intersection <strong>from a random direction.</strong></li>
<li><strong><code>Esc</code> Escape:</strong> ends the simulation.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">It must not be possible to use the keyboard to spam the creation of vehicles; they must be created with a safe distance between them.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">A safe distance is any distance which enables the vehicles to avoid crashing into each other.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example</h3><a id="user-content-example" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example" href="#example"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can see an example for road_intersection <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6B0-ZBET6mo" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</p>
